class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_18  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light"><div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p style="text-align: center;">DIAMO LUCE ALLE TUE IDEE</p><h2 style="text-align: center;">Il nostro Blog illuminante</h2></div></div><div class="et_pb_module dsm_blog_carousel dsm_blog_carousel_0"><div class="et_pb_module_inner"><div class="dsm-blog-carousel" data-orientation='horizontal' data-loop='1' data-speed='500' data-columnsdesktop='3' data-columnsphone='1' data-columnstablet='2' data-autoplay='on' data-autoplayspeed='5000' data-ordernumber='0' data-autoplay-viewport='80%'><div class="swiper-container dsm_blog_carousel_wrapper" dir="ltr"><div class="dsm-blog-carousel-wrapper swiper-wrapper"><article class="dsm-blog-carousel-item swiper-slide"><div class="dsm-grid-post-holder-inner"><div class="dsm-entry-image"><div class="dsm-entry-thumbnail"> <a href="https://ideadiluce.com/2024/06/26/luce-calda-o-fredda/"> <img class="dsm-entry-header"><h2 class="dsm-entry-title"> <a href="https://ideadiluce.com/2024/06/26/luce-calda-o-fredda/">Luce CALDA o FREDDA: la scelta illuminante</a></h2></header><div class="dsm-entry-meta"> <span class="dsm-meta-seperator">|</span> <span class="dsm-posted-on"><time datetime="Giu 26, 2024">Giu 26, 2024</time></span> <span class="dsm-meta-seperator">|</span> <span class="dsm-posted-category"><a href="https://ideadiluce.com/category/look/" rel="tag">SHOP THE LOOK</a></span></div><div class="dsm-entry-content"><div class="dsm-post-excerpt"><p>Giochi di ruolo. L\&#039;illuminazione gioca un ruolo fondamentale nel creare l\&#039;atmosfera perfetta in ogni ambiente della nostra casa. Ma come scegliere tra luce calda e fredda? Scopriamolo&hellip;</p></div></div><div class="dsm-readmore-wrap et_pb_bg_layout_light"> <a href="https://ideadiluce.com/2024/06/26/luce-calda-o-fredda/"  class="dsm-readmore-btn  et_pb_custom_button_icon" data-icon="5" target="">LEGGI TUTTO</a></div></div></div></article><article class="dsm-blog-carousel-item swiper-slide"><div class="dsm-grid-post-holder-inner"><div class="dsm-entry-image"><div class="dsm-entry-thumbnail"> <a href="https://ideadiluce.com/2024/06/25/la-natura-trend-2024/"> <img decoding="async" width="1080" height="338" src="https://ideadiluce.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/06/copertina.jpg" class="skip-lazy wp-post-image" alt="" srcset="https://ideadiluce.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/06/copertina-980x306.jpg 980w, https://ideadiluce.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/06/copertina-480x150.jpg 480w" sizes="(min-width: 0px) and (max-width: 480px) 480px, (min-width: 481px) and (max-width: 980px) 980px, (min-width: 981px) 1080px, 100vw" /> </a></div></div><div class="dsm-entry-wrapper"><header class="dsm-entry-header"><h2 class="dsm-entry-title"> <a href="https://ideadiluce.com/2024/06/25/la-natura-trend-2024/">Lighting trends 2024 &#8211; LA NATURA</a></h2></header><div class="dsm-entry-meta"> <span class="dsm-meta-seperator">|</span> <span class="dsm-posted-on"><time datetime="Giu 25, 2024">Giu 25, 2024</time></span> <span class="dsm-meta-seperator">|</span> <span class="dsm-posted-category"><a href="https://ideadiluce.com/category/style/" rel="tag">STYLE RADAR</a></span></div><div class="dsm-entry-content"><div class="dsm-post-excerpt"><p>La natura entra in casa. La natura è la musa ispiratrice del design 2024, e l\&#039;illuminazione non fa eccezione. Ispirandosi alla bellezza di alveari, al flusso dell\&#039;acqua&hellip;</p></div></div><div class="dsm-readmore-wrap et_pb_bg_layout_light"> <a href="https://ideadiluce.com/2024/06/25/la-natura-trend-2024/"  class="dsm-readmore-btn  et_pb_custom_button_icon" data-icon="5" target="">LEGGI TUTTO</a></div></div></div></article><article class="dsm-blog-carousel-item swiper-slide"><div class="dsm-grid-post-holder-inner"><div class="dsm-entry-image"><div class="dsm-entry-thumbnail"> <a href="https://ideadiluce.com/2024/06/04/calipso-artemide-io-vengo-dalla-luna/"> <img decoding="async" width="1080" height="338" src="https://ideadiluce.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/06/calispo-up2.jpg" class="skip-lazy wp-post-image" alt="" srcset="https://ideadiluce.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/06/calispo-up2-980x306.jpg 980w, https://ideadiluce.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/06/calispo-up2-480x150.jpg 480w" sizes="(min-width: 0px) and (max-width: 480px) 480px, (min-width: 481px) and (max-width: 980px) 980px, (min-width: 981px) 1080px, 100vw" /> </a></div></div><div class="dsm-entry-wrapper"><header class="dsm-entry-header"><h2 class="dsm-entry-title"> <a href="https://ideadiluce.com/2024/06/04/calipso-artemide-io-vengo-dalla-luna/">CALIPSO &#8211; Designed by Artemide</a></h2></header><div class="dsm-entry-meta"> <span class="dsm-meta-seperator">|</span> <span class="dsm-posted-on"><time datetime="Giu 4, 2024">Giu 4, 2024</time></span> <span class="dsm-meta-seperator">|</span> <span class="dsm-posted-category"><a href="https://ideadiluce.com/category/design/" rel="tag">DESIGN SPOTLIGHT</a></span></div><div class="dsm-entry-content"><div class="dsm-post-excerpt"><p>Io vengo dalla luna. Un\&#039;emozione luminosa prende forma con Artemide Calipso, un\&#039;opera d\&#039;arte di design che cattura la bellezza lunare.
